63	   The patterns are used inside ``[ ]`` in regular expressions.
64	
65	   Rule (5) requires determination of matching open/close pairs. However, the
66	   pairing of open/close quotes is ambiguous due to  different typographic
67	   conventions in different languages. The ``quote_pairs`` function tests
68	   whether two characters form an open/close pair.
69	
70	   The patterns are generated by

72	   on the Python version and avoid the time-consuming generation with every
73	   Docutils run. See there for motives and implementation details.

76	   Unicode standard. The current lists are generated with the help of the
77	   "unicodedata" module of Python %(python_version)s (based on Unicode version %(unidata_version)s).
78	
79	   .. _inline markup recognition rules:
80	      https://docutils.sourceforge.io/docs/ref/rst/restructuredtext.html
81	      #inline-markup-recognition-rules

114	def match_chars(c1, c2):
115	    """Test whether `c1` and `c2` are a matching open/close character pair."""
